Security结合OAuth2</h2> <h3>1.依赖</h3> <pre><code> </code></pre> 2020-05-18T15:10:00+08:06/Xuxx_Blogs/archives/bj23/Spring Boot整合Swagger2020-07-01T17:18:24.565344+00:00Xuxxxuxx3319@gmail.com暂无<h2>1. Swagger简介</h2> <p><strong>前后端分离</strong></p> <ul> <li>前端 -&gt; 前端控制层、视图层</li> <li>后端 -&gt; 后端控制层、服务层、数据访问层</li> <li>前后端通过API进行交互</li> <li>前后端相对独立且松耦合</li> </ul> <p><strong>产生的问题</strong></p> <ul> <li>前后端集成，前端或者后端无法做到“及时协商，尽早解决”，最终导致问题集中爆发</li> </ul> <p><strong>解决方案</strong></p> <ul> <li>首先定义schema [ 计划的提纲 ]，并实时跟踪最新的API，降低集成风险</li> </ul> <p><strong>Swagger</strong></p> <ul> <li>号称世界上最流行的API框架</li> <li>Restful Api 文档在线自动生成器 =&gt; <strong>API 文档 与API 定义同步更新</strong></li> <li>直接运行，在线测试API</li> <li>支持多种语言 （如：Java，PHP等）</li> <li>官网：<a href="https://swagger.io/">https://swagger.io/</a></li> </ul> <h2>2. Spring Boot集成Swagger</h2> <p><strong>Spring Boot集成Swagger</strong> -&gt; <strong>springfox</strong>，两个jar包</p> <ul> <li><strong>Springfox-swagger2</strong></li> <li><strong>swagger-springmvc</strong></li> </ul> <p><strong>使用Swagger</strong></p> <p>要求：jdk 1.8 + 否则swagger2无法运行</p> <p>步骤：</p> <p>1、新建一个Spring Boot-web项目</p> <p>2、添加Maven依赖</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c">&lt;!-- https://mvnrepository.com/artifact/io.springfox/springfox-swagger2 --&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;dependency&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;groupId&gt;</span>io.springfox<span class="nt">&lt;/groupId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;artifactId&gt;</span>springfox-swagger2<span class="nt">&lt;/artifactId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;version&gt;</span>2.9.2<span class="nt">&lt;/version&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;/dependency&gt;</span> <span class="c">&lt;!-- https://mvnrepository.com/artifact/io.springfox/springfox-swagger-ui --&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;dependency&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;groupId&gt;</span>io.springfox<span class="nt">&lt;/groupId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;artifactId&gt;</span>springfox-swagger-ui<span class="nt">&lt;/artifactId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;version&gt;</span>2.9.2<span class="nt">&lt;/version&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;/dependency&gt;</span> </pre></div> <p>3、编写HelloController，测试确保运行成功！</p> <p>4、要使用Swagger，需要编写一个配置类-SwaggerConfig来配置 Swagger</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@Configuration</span> <span class="nd">@EnableSwagger2</span><span class="c1">// 开启Swagger2</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">SwaggerConfig</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>5、访问测试 ：<a href="http://localhost:8080/swagger-ui.html">http://localhost:8080/swagger-ui.html</a> ，可以看到swagger的界面；</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 119.63840399002494" data-width="1919" data-height="802"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/ec355bdb47aa00f17b401e61ffa5c79b.png" alt="" /></figure></p> <h2>3. 配置Swagger</h2> <p>1、Swagger实例Bean是Docket，所以通过配置Docket实例来配置Swaggger。</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="c1">//配置docket以配置Swagger具体参数</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>2、可以通过apiInfo()属性配置文档信息</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//配置API描述信息&gt;&gt;&gt;ApiInfo</span> <span class="kd">private</span> <span class="n">ApiInfo</span> <span class="nf">apiInfo</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="c1">//作者信息</span> <span class="n">Contact</span> <span class="n">contact</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Contact</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;Xuxx&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;暂无&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;xuxx3319@gmail.com&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">ApiInfo</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="s">&quot;API信息&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;ApI描述&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;v1.0&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;服务条款网址&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">contact</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;Apache 2.0&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">ArrayList</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">VendorExtension</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="p">());</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>3、Docket 实例关联上 apiInfo()</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//配置Swagger的Docket</span> <span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apiInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">apiInfo</span><span class="p">());</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>4、重启项目，访问测试 <a href="http://localhost:8080/swagger-ui.html">http://localhost:8080/swagger-ui.html</a> 看下效果；</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 109.96563573883161" data-width="1920" data-height="873"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/08e0001208af5daae27382acfb5f728c.png" alt="" /></figure></p> <h2>4. 配置扫描接口</h2> <p>1、构建Docket时通过select()方法配置怎么扫描接口。</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//配置Swagger的Docket</span> <span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apiInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">apiInfo</span><span class="p">())</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">select</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1">//RequestHandlerSelectors 配置要扫描的接口</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apis</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">RequestHandlerSelectors</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basePackage</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;com.xuxx.swagger.controller&quot;</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">build</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>2、重启项目测试，由于配置根据包的路径扫描接口，所以只能看到一个类</p> <p>3、除了通过包路径配置扫描接口外，还可以通过配置其他方式扫描接口，这里注释一下所有的配置方式：</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//any:扫描全部</span> <span class="c1">//none:全部不扫描</span> <span class="c1">//basePackage:指定要扫描的包 </span> <span class="c1">//withMethodAnnotation:扫描带注解的方法,例:withMethodAnnotation(GetMapping.class)</span> <span class="c1">//withClassAnnotation:扫描带注解的类,例:withClassAnnotation(RestController.class)</span> </pre></div> <p>4、除此之外，还可以配置接口扫描过滤：</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apiInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">apiInfo</span><span class="p">())</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">select</span><span class="p">()</span><span class="c1">// select():配置扫描接口, RequestHandlerSelectors:配置如何扫描接口</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apis</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">RequestHandlerSelectors</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basePackage</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;com.xuxx.swagger.controller&quot;</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="c1">//配置如何通过path过滤,即这里只扫描请求以&#39;/api/&#39;为前缀的接口</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">paths</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">PathSelectors</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">ant</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;/api/**&quot;</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">build</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>5、这里的可选值还有</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="n">any</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1">//任何请求都扫描</span> <span class="n">none</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1">//任何请求都不扫描</span> <span class="n">regex</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">pathRegex</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">//通过正则表达式控制</span> <span class="n">ant</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">antPattern</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">//通过ant()匹配</span> </pre></div> <h2>5. 配置Swagger开关</h2> <p>1、通过enable()方法配置是否启用swagger，如果为false，则不能访问swagger</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apiInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">apiInfo</span><span class="p">())</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">enable</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">//配置是否启用swagger，如果是false，则不能访问swagger</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">select</span><span class="p">()</span><span class="c1">// select():配置扫描接口, RequestHandlerSelectors:配置如何扫描接口</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apis</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">RequestHandlerSelectors</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basePackage</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;com.xuxx.swagger.controller&quot;</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="c1">//配置如何通过path过滤,即这里只扫描请求以&#39;/api/&#39;为前缀的接口</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">paths</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">PathSelectors</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">ant</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;/api/**&quot;</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">build</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>2、如何动态配置当项目处于dev、test环境时使用swagger，处于prod时不显示？</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="c1">//environment:表示当前应用程序运行的环境的接口。</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Environment</span> <span class="n">environment</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="c1">//配置要使用swagger的环境</span> <span class="n">Profiles</span> <span class="n">profiles</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Profiles</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">of</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;dev&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;test&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//判断当前是否处于该环境</span> <span class="c1">//通过enable()接收此参数判断是否使用swagger</span> <span class="kt">boolean</span> <span class="n">flag</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">environment</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">acceptsProfiles</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">profiles</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apiInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">apiInfo</span><span class="p">())</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">enable</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">flag</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">//配置是否启用swagger，如果是false，在浏览器将无法访问</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">select</span><span class="p">()</span><span class="c1">// 通过.select()方法，去配置扫描接口,RequestHandlerSelectors配置如何扫描接口</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apis</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">RequestHandlerSelectors</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basePackage</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;com.xuxx.swagger.controller&quot;</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="c1">//配置如何通过path过滤,即这里只扫描请求以&#39;/api/&#39;为前缀的接口</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">paths</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">PathSelectors</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">ant</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;/api/**&quot;</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">build</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>3、可以在项目中增加一个dev的配置文件查看效果！</p> <p>application.properties</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="na">spring.profiles.active</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s">dev</span> </pre></div> <p>application-dev.properties</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="na">server.port</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s">8081</span> </pre></div> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 145.7886676875957" data-width="1904" data-height="653"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/9ea05279d2ed4fc2a7ddb7eec4e00242.png" alt="" /></figure></p> <p>如果环境不是<code>dev</code>或者<code>test</code>,swagger便关闭。</p> <h2>6. 配置API分组</h2> <p>1、如果没有配置分组，默认是default。通过groupName()方法即可配置分组：</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Environment</span> <span class="n">environment</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">apiInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">apiInfo</span><span class="p">())</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="na">groupName</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;A&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">// 配置分组</span> <span class="c1">// 省略....</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>2、重启项目查看分组</p> <p>3、如何配置多个分组？配置多个分组只需要配置多个docket即可：</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket1</span><span class="p">(){</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="na">groupName</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;A&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="nd">@Bean</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">Docket</span> <span class="nf">docket2</span><span class="p">(){</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">Docket</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DocumentationType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">SWAGGER_2</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="na">groupName</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;B&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>4、重启项目查看即可</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 127.82956058588549" data-width="1920" data-height="751"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/5b98ef7984dfbf5c80d54d37e21463c1.png" alt="" /></figure></p> <h2>7. 实体配置</h2> <p>1、新建一个实体类</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@ApiModel</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;用户实体类-user&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">User</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="nd">@ApiModelProperty</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;用户名&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">username</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nd">@ApiModelProperty</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;密码&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">password</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>2、只要这个实体在<strong>请求接口</strong>的返回值上（即使是泛型），都能映射到实体项中：</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@GetMapping</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;/getUser&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">User</span> <span class="nf">getUser</span><span class="p">(){</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">User</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>3、重启查看测试</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 270.80924855491327" data-width="1874" data-height="346"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/e5824d7ab3a687391ffda24b9c3ef7af.png" alt="" /></figure></p> <p>注：并不是因为@ApiModel这个注解让实体显示在这里了，而是只要出现在接口方法的返回值上的实体都会显示在这里，而@ApiModel和@ApiModelProperty这两个注解只是为实体添加注释的。</p> <ul> <li>@ApiModel为类添加注释</li> </ul> <ul> <li>@ApiModelProperty为类属性添加注释</li> </ul> <h2>8. 常用注解</h2> <p>Swagger的所有注解定义在io.swagger.annotations包下</p> <p>下面列一些经常用到的，未列举出来的可以另行查阅说明：</p> <table> <thead><tr> <th>Swagger注解</th> <th>简单说明</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody> <tr> <td>@Api(tags = "xxx模块说明")</td> <td>作用在模块类上,为接口添加标签</td> </tr> <tr> <td>@ApiOperation(vale="xxx接口说明"，tags="xxx"，notes="接口的详细描述")</td> <td>作用在接口方法上,vale:添加说明,tage:添加标签</td> </tr> <tr> <td>@ApiModel("xxxPOJO说明")</td> <td>作用在模型类上：如VO、BO</td> </tr> <tr> <td>@ApiModelProperty(value = "xxx属性说明",hidden = true)</td> <td>作用在类方法和属性上，hidden设置为true可以隐藏该属性</td> </tr> <tr> <td>@ApiParam("xxx参数说明")</td> <td>作用在参数、方法和字段上，类似@ApiModelProperty</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <p>也可以给请求的接口配置一些注释</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@ApiOperation</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">value</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s">&quot;api接口-getUsername&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">tags</span> <span class="o">=</span><span class="s">&quot;属于xxx的接口&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">notes</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s">&quot;接口的详细描述&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="nd">@PostMapping</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;/getUsername&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="nd">@ResponseBody</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="nf">getUsername</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nd">@ApiParam</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;这个username会被返回&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">username</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">username</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <p>这样的话，可以给一些比较难理解的属性或者接口，增加一些配置信息，让人更容易阅读！</p> <p>相较于传统的Postman或Curl方式测试接口，使用swagger简直就是傻瓜式操作，不需要额外说明文档(写得好本身就是文档)而且更不容易出错，只需要录入数据然后点击Execute，如果再配合自动化框架，可以说基本就不需要人为操作了。</p> <p>Swagger是个优秀的工具，现在国内已经有很多的中小型互联网公司都在使用它，相较于传统的要先出Word接口文档再测试的方式，显然这样也更符合现在的快速迭代开发行情。当然了，提醒下大家在正式环境要记得关闭Swagger，一来出于安全考虑，二来也可以节省运行时内存。</p> <h2>拓展：其他皮肤</h2> <p>可以导入不同的包实现不同的皮肤定义：</p> <p>1、默认的 class="nt">&lt;artifactId&gt;</span>swagger-mg-ui<span class="nt">&lt;/artifactId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;version&gt;</span>1.0.6<span class="nt">&lt;/version&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;/dependency&gt;</span> </pre></div> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 190.47619047619048" data-width="1920" data-height="504"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/69d2f605e680bd7eae5ef85c2f353794.png" alt="" /></figure></p> 2020-05-27T23:50:00+08:06/Xuxx_Blogs/archives/bj24/RibbitMQ实战教程2020-07-01T17:18:24.565323+00:00Xuxxxuxx3319@gmail.com暂无<h2>1.MQ引言</h2> <h3>1.1 什么是MQ</h3> <p><code>MQ</code>(Message Quene) : 翻译为 <code>消息队列</code>,通过典型的 <code>生产者</code>和<code>消费者</code>模型,生产者不断向消息队列中生产消息，消费者不断的从队列中获取消息。因为消息的生产和消费都是异步的，而且只关心消息的发送和接收，没有业务逻辑的侵入,轻松的实现系统间解耦。别名为 <code>消息中间件</code> 通过利用高效可靠的消息传递机制进行平台无关的数据交流，并基于数据通信来进行分布式系统的集成。</p> <h3>1.2 MQ有哪些</h3> <p>当今市面上有很多主流的消息中间件，如老牌的<code>ActiveMQ</code>、<code>RabbitMQ</code>，炙手可热的<code>Kafka</code>，阿里巴巴自主开发<code>RocketMQ</code>等。</p> <h3>1.3 不同MQ特点</h3> <pre><code># 1.ActiveMQ ActiveMQ 是Apache出品，最流行的，能力强劲的开源消息总线。它是一个完全支持JMS规范的的消息中间件。丰富的API,多种集群架构模式让ActiveMQ在业界成为老牌的消息中间件,在中小型企业颇受欢迎! # 2.Kafka Kafka是LinkedIn开源的分布式发布-订阅消息系统，目前归属于Apache顶级项目。Kafka主要特点是基于Pull的模式来处理消息消费， 追求高吞吐量，一开始的目的就是用于日志收集和传输。0.8版本开始支持复制，不支持事务，对消息的重复、丢失、错误没有严格要求， 适合产生大量数据的互联网服务的数据收集业务。 # 3.RocketMQ RocketMQ是阿里开源的消息中间件，它是纯Java开发，具有高吞吐量、高可用性、适合大规模分布式系统应用的特点。RocketMQ思路起 源于Kafka，但并不是Kafka的一个Copy，它对消息的可靠传输及事务性做了优化，目前在阿里集团被广泛应用于交易、充值、流计算、消 息推送、日志流式处理、binglog分发等场景。 # 4.RabbitMQ RabbitMQ是使用Erlang语言开发的开源消息队列系统，基于AMQP协议来实现。AMQP的主要特征是面向消息、队列、路由（包括点对点和 发布/订阅）、可靠性、安全。AMQP协议更多用在企业系统内对数据一致性、稳定性和可靠性要求很高的场景，对性能和吞吐量的要求还在 其次。</code></pre> <blockquote><p>RabbitMQ比Kafka可靠，Kafka更适合IO高吞吐的处理，一般应用在大数据日志处理或对实时性（少量延迟），可靠性（少量丢数据）要求稍低的场景使用，比如ELK日志收集。</p> </blockquote> <hr> <h2>2.RabbitMQ 的引言</h2> <h3>2.1 RabbitMQ</h3> <blockquote><p>基于<code>AMQP</code>协议，erlang语言开发，是部署最广泛的开源消息中间件,是最受欢迎的开源消息中间件之一。</p> </blockquote> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 87.60162601626017" data-width="2586" data-height="1476"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/768832c026023439932cf76fa1c05b88.png" alt="image-20190925215603036" /><figcaption>image-20190925215603036</figcaption></figure></p> <p><code>官网</code>: <a href="https://www.rabbitmq.com/">https://www.rabbitmq.com/</a></p> <p><code>官方教程</code>: <a href="https://www.rabbitmq.com/#getstarted">https://www.rabbitmq.com/#getstarted</a></p> <pre><code> # AMQP 协议 AMQP（advanced message queuing protocol）`在2003年时被提出，最早用于解决金融领不同平台之间的消息传递交互问题。顾名思义，AMQP是一种协议，更准确的说是一种binary wire-level protocol（链接协议）。这是其和JMS的本质差别，AMQP不从API层进行限定，而是直接定义网络交换的数据格式。这使得实现了AMQP的provider天然性就是跨平台的。以下是AMQP协议模型:</code></pre> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 123.42799188640974" data-width="1217" data-height="493"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/9ef65242b80e1ebc1d73f53ed50086a4.png" alt="" /></figure></p> <h3>2.2 RabbitMQ 的安装</h3> <h4>2.2.1 下载</h4> <p><code>官网下载地址</code>: <a href="https://www.rabbitmq.com/download.html![image-20190925220115235](..\static\笔记图片\RibbitMQ\image-20190925220115235.png">https://www.rabbitmq.com/download.html![image-20190925220115235](..\static\笔记图片\RibbitMQ\image-20190925220115235.png</a>)</p> <blockquote><p><code>最新版本</code>: 3.7.18</p> </blockquote> <h4>2.2.2 下载的安装包<figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 478.0487804878049" data-width="1568" data-height="164"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/4dd564f0437ff4a3ef3c7960342d835c.png" alt="image-20190925220343521" /><figcaption>image-20190925220343521</figcaption></figure></h4> <blockquote><p><code>注意</code>:这里的安装包是centos7安装的包</p> </blockquote> <h4>2.2.3 安装步骤</h4> <pre><code># 1.将rabbitmq安装包上传到linux系统中 erlang-22.0.7-1.el7.x86_64.rpm rabbitmq-server-3.7.18-1.el7.noarch.rpm # 2.安装Erlang依赖包 rpm -ivh erlang-22.0.7-1.el7.x86_64.rpm # 3.安装RabbitMQ安装包(需要联网) yum install -y rabbitmq-server-3.7.18-1.el7.noarch.rpm 注意:默认安装完成后配置文件模板在:/usr/share/doc/rabbitmq-server-3.7.18/rabbitmq.config.example目录中,需要 将配置文件复制到/etc/rabbitmq/目录中,并修改名称为rabbitmq.config # 4.复制配置文件 cp /usr/share/doc/rabbitmq-server-3.7.18/rabbitmq.config.example /etc/rabbitmq/rabbitmq.config # 5.查看配置文件位置 ls /etc/rabbitmq/rabbitmq.config # 6.修改配置文件(参见下图:) vim /etc/rabbitmq/rabbitmq.config</code></pre> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 244.23963133640552" data-width="2120" data-height="434"><img /><figcaption>image-20190925222230260</figcaption></figure></p> <p>将上图中配置文件中红色部分去掉<code>%%</code>,以及最后的<code>,</code>逗号 修改为下图:</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 358.44594594594594" /><figcaption>image-20190925222329200</figcaption></figure></p> <pre><code># 7.执行如下命令,启动rabbitmq中的插件管理 rabbitmq-plugins enable rabbitmq_management 出现如下说明: Enabling plugins on node rabbit@localhost: rabbitmq_management The following plugins have been configured: rabbitmq_management rabbitmq_management_agent rabbitmq_web_dispatch Applying plugin configuration to rabbit@localhost... Offline change; changes will take effect at broker restart. # 8.启动RabbitMQ的服务 systemctl start rabbitmq-server systemctl restart rabbitmq-server systemctl stop rabbitmq-server # 9.查看服务状态(见下图:) systemctl status rabbitmq-server ● rabbitmq-server.service - RabbitMQ broker Loaded: loaded (/usr/lib/systemd/system/rabbitmq-server.service; disabled; vendor preset: disabled) Active: active (running) since 三 2019-09-25 22:26:35 CST; 7s ago Main PID: 2904 (beam.smp) Status: "Initialized" CGroup: /system.slice/rabbitmq-server.service ├─2904 /usr/lib64/erlang/erts-10.4.4/bin/beam.smp -W w -A 64 -MBas ageffcbf -MHas ageffcbf - MBlmbcs... ├─3220 erl_child_setup 32768 ├─3243 inet_gethost 4 └─3244 inet_gethost 4 .........</code></pre> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 82.46951219512195" data-width="3246" data-height="1968"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/f2be7a0ae07763b79a893a2c6b61d404.png" alt="image-20190925222743776" /><figcaption>image-20190925222743776</figcaption></figure></p> <pre><code># 10.关闭防火墙服务 systemctl disable firewalld Removed syamlink /etc/systemd/system/multi-user.target.wants/firewalld.service. Removed syamlink /etc/systemd/system/dbus-org.fedoraproject.FirewallD1.service. systemctl stop firewalld # 11.访问web管理界面 http://10.15.0.8:15672/</code></pre> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 221.79054054054055" data-width="2626" data-height="592"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/fa9424976bd1e88efcdd268ebc8c5001.png" alt="image-20190926194738708" /><figcaption>image-20190926194738708</figcaption></figure></p> <pre><code># 12.登录管理界面 username: guest password: guest</code></pre> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 98.342939481268" data-width="2730" data-height="1388"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/2d5da6c6b8bf716d77efae35d336a115.png" alt="image-20190926194954822" /><figcaption>image-20190926194954822</figcaption></figure></p> <hr> <h2>3. RabiitMQ 配置</h2> <h3>3.1RabbitMQ 管理命令行</h3> <pre><code># 1.服务启动相关 systemctl start|restart|stop|status rabbitmq-server # 2.管理命令行 用来在不使用web管理界面情况下命令操作RabbitMQ rabbitmqctl help 可以查看更多命令 # 3.插件管理命令行 rabbitmq-plugins enable|list|disable</code></pre> <h3>3.2 web管理界面介绍</h3> <h4>3.2.1 overview概览</h4> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 111.92080876158383" data-width="2657" data-height="1187"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/b0418696e5653ec1ad90f52af9efd25a.png" alt="image-20191126162026720" /><figcaption>image-20191126162026720</figcaption></figure></p> <ul> <li><p><code>connections：无论生产者还是消费者，都需要与RabbitMQ建立连接后才可以完成消息的生产和消费，在这里可以查看连接情况</code></p> </li> <li><p><code>channels：通道，建立连接后，会形成通道，消息的投递获取依赖通道。</code></p> </li> <li><p><code>Exchanges：交换机，用来实现消息的路由</code></p> </li> <li><p><code>Queues：队列，即消息队列，消息存放在队列中，等待消费，消费后被移除队列。</code></p> </li> </ul> <h4>3.2.2 Admin用户和虚拟主机管理</h4> <h5>1. 添加用户</h5> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 215.75121163166398" data-width="2671" data-height="619"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/4121e483f4e3f71bbbe09d624fd406cc.png" alt="image-20191126162617280" /><figcaption>image-20191126162617280</figcaption></figure></p> <p>上面的Tags选项，其实是指定用户的角色，可选的有以下几个：</p> <ul> <li><p><code>超级管理员(administrator)</code></p> <p>可登陆管理控制台，可查看所有的信息，并且可以对用户，策略(policy)进行操作。</p> </li> <li><p><code>监控者(monitoring)</code></p> <p>可登陆管理控制台，同时可以查看rabbitmq节点的相关信息(进程数，内存使用情况，磁盘使用情况等)</p> </li> <li><p><code>策略制定者(policymaker)</code></p> <p>可登陆管理控制台, 同时可以对policy进行管理。但无法查看节点的相关信息(上图红框标识的部分)。</p> </li> <li><p><code>普通管理者(management)</code></p> <p>仅可登陆管理控制台，无法看到节点信息，也无法对策略进行管理。</p> </li> <li><p><code>其他</code></p> <p>无法登陆管理控制台，通常就是普通的生产者和消费者。</p> </li> </ul> <h5>2. 创建虚拟主机</h5> <pre><code># 虚拟主机 为了让各个用户可以互不干扰的工作，RabbitMQ添加了虚拟主机（Virtual Hosts）的概念。其实就是一个独立的访问路径，不同用户使用不同路径，各自有自己的队列、交换机，互相不会影响。</code></pre> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 275.0" data-width="2651" data-height="482"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/4a6f6e328da79eaaf8823b2b7476e8a3.png" alt="image-20191126163023153" /><figcaption>image-20191126163023153</figcaption></figure></p> <h5>3. 绑定虚拟主机和用户</h5> <p>创建好虚拟主机，我们还要给用户添加访问权限：</p> <p>点击添加好的虚拟主机：</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 309.05882352941177" data-width="2627" data-height="425"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/0ea5750a4b74193ba2fd3c1df75850c2.png" alt="image-20191126163506795" /><figcaption>image-20191126163506795</figcaption></figure></p> <p>进入虚拟机设置界面:</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 121.84014869888476" data-width="2622" data-height="1076"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/f83a3112ad19417e8a9de04673e4c3ef.png" alt="image-20191126163631889" /><figcaption>image-20191126163631889</figcaption></figure></p> <hr> <h2>4.RabbitMQ 的第一个程序</h2> <h3>4.0 AMQP协议的回顾</h3> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 179.20604914933838" data-width="1896" data-height="529"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/2c0402a64943df3ea1edf391d5bdfaa2.png" alt="image-20200312140114784" /><figcaption>image-20200312140114784</figcaption></figure></p> <h3>4.1 RabbitMQ支持的消息模型</h3> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 100.83333333333333" data-width="3146" data-height="1560"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/5f0b0986e26e72ab7a05f17ae78e93ad.png" alt="image-20191126165434784" /><figcaption>image-20191126165434784</figcaption></figure></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 100.97402597402598" data-width="3110" data-height="1540"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/ab8610f1223d604017a491346f3c0435.png" alt="image-20191126165459282" /><figcaption>image-20191126165459282</figcaption></figure></p> <h3>4.2 引入依赖</h3> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nt">&lt;dependency&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;groupId&gt;</span>com.rabbitmq<span class="nt">&lt;/groupId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;artifactId&gt;</span>amqp-client<span class="nt">&lt;/artifactId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;version&gt;</span>5.7.2<span class="nt">&lt;/version&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;/dependency&gt;</span> </pre></div> <h3>4.3 第一种模型(直连)</h3> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 337.0860927152318" data-width="1018" data-height="151"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/208409a80ad47ab5310b8b7da055cc86.png" alt="" /></figure></p> <p>在上图的模型中，有以下概念：</p> <ul> <li>P：生产者，也就是要发送消息的程序</li> <li>C：消费者：消息的接受者，会一直等待消息到来。</li> <li>queue：消息队列，图中红色部分。类似一个邮箱，可以缓存消息；生产者向其中投递消息，消费者从其中取出消息。</li> </ul> <h5>1. 开发生产者</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//创建连接工厂</span> <span class="n">ConnectionFactory</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">ConnectionFactory</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//设置连接rabbitmq主机</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">setHost</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;192.168.123.128&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//设置连接端口号</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">setPort</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">5672</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//设置连接的虚拟主机(自己创建的)</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">setUsername</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;ems&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//设置连接的虚拟主机的用户名和密码</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">setPassword</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;123&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">setVirtualHost</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;/ems&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//创建连接对象</span> <span class="n">Connection</span> <span class="n">connection</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">newConnection</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//创建通道</span> <span class="n">Channel</span> <span class="n">channel</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">connection</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">createChannel</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//将通道绑定到队列上</span> <span class="c1">//参数1 queue:队列名称(如果不存在则自动创建) 参数2 durable:持久化队列，则为true。参数3 exclusive:独占队列，则为true。参数4 autoDelete:是否在消费完成后自动删除队列，是则为true。参数5 arguments:队列的其他附件参数</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//发布消息(此时没有使用交换机)</span> <span class="c1">//参数1: 交换机名称 参数2:队列名称 参数3 :传递消息额外设置 参数4 :消息的具体内容</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicPublish</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;hello rabbitmq&quot;</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">getBytes</span><span class="p">());</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">close</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="n">connection</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">close</span><span class="p">();</span> </pre></div> <h5>2. 开发消费者</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//创建连接工厂</span> <span class="n">ConnectionFactory</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">ConnectionFactory</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//设置连接rabbitmq主机</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="s">&quot;ems&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//设置连接的虚拟主机的用户名和密码</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">setPassword</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;123&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">setVirtualHost</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;/ems&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//创建连接对象</span> <span class="n">Connection</span> <span class="n">connection</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">connectionFactory</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">newConnection</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//创建通道</span> <span class="n">Channel</span> <span class="n">channel</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">connection</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">createChannel</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//将通道绑定到队列上</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//消费消息</span> <span class="c1">//参数1:queue—队列的名称</span> <span class="c1">//参数2:autoAck—开启消息的自动确认机制</span> <span class="c1">//参数3:callback—消费时回调接口</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicConsume</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">DefaultConsumer</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="nd">@Override</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>3. 参数说明</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="n">参数1</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">用来声明通道对应的队列</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">如果不存在则自动创建</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="n">参数2</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">用来指定是否持久化队列</span> <span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="n">参数3</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">用来指定是否独占队列</span> <span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="n">参数4</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">用来指定是否自动删除队列</span> <span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="n">参数5</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">对队列的额外配置</span> <span class="c1">//消费者需要和生产者绑定一样的队列上才能进行</span> </pre></div> <hr> <h3>4.4 第二种模型(work quene)</h3> <p><code>Work queues</code>，也被称为（<code>Task queues</code>），任务模型。当消息处理比较耗时的时候，可能生产消息的速度会远远大于消息的消费速度。长此以往，消息就会堆积越来越多，无法及时处理。此时就可以使用work 模型：<strong>让多个消费者绑定到一个队列，共同消费队列中的消息</strong>。队列中的消息一旦消费，就会消失，因此任务是不会被重复执行的。</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 359.92063492063494" data-width="1814" data-height="252"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/f3eba840cae99216c59e99ff41cfc82e.png" alt="image-20200314221002008" /><figcaption>image-20200314221002008</figcaption></figure></p> <p>角色：</p> <ul> <li>P：生产者：任务的发布者</li> <li>C1：消费者-1，领取任务并完成任务，假设完成速度较慢</li> <li>C2：消费者-2：领取任务并完成任务，假设完成速度较快</li> </ul> <h5>1. 开发生产者</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">++</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicPublish</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="s">&quot;====&gt;:我是消息&quot;</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="na">getBytes</span><span class="p">());</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> <h5>2.开发消费者-1</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicConsume</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">DefaultConsumer</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="nd">@Override</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Envelope</span> <span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">AMQP</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">BasicProperties</span> <span class="n">properties</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者1: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>3.开发消费者-2</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicConsume</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">DefaultConsumer</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="nd">@Override</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Envelope</span> <span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">AMQP</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">BasicProperties</span> <span class="n">properties</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="k">try</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">Thread</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">sleep</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1000</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//处理消息比较慢 一秒处理一个消息</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="k">catch</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">InterruptedException</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">printStackTrace</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者2: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>4.测试结果</h5> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 540.4494382022472" data-width="1924" data-height="178"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/21b0133a0bbab3ef50a2b646a6cb5753.png" alt="image-20200314223242058" /><figcaption>image-20200314223242058</figcaption></figure></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 603.6312849162011" data-width="2161" data-height="179"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/487e46633ef6fd87ebee9d60d386814e.png" alt="image-20200314223302207" /><figcaption>image-20200314223302207</figcaption></figure></p> <blockquote><p><code>总结:默认情况下，RabbitMQ将按顺序将每个消息发送给下一个使用者。平均而言，每个消费者都会收到相同数量的消息。这种分发消息的方式称为循环。</code><a href="https://www.rabbitmq.com/tutorials/tutorial-two-java.html">官方文档</a></p> </blockquote> <h5>5.消息自动确认机制</h5> <blockquote><p>Doing a task can take a few seconds. You may wonder what happens if one of the consumers starts a long task and dies with it only partly done. With our current code, once RabbitMQ delivers a message to the consumer it immediately marks it for deletion. In this case, if you kill a worker we will lose the message it was just processing. We'll also lose all the messages that were dispatched to this particular worker but were not yet handled.</p> <p>But we don't want to lose any tasks. If a worker dies, we'd like the task to be delivered to another worker.</p> </blockquote> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicQos</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">);</span><span class="c1">//一次只接受一条未确认的消息</span> <span class="c1">//参数2:关闭自动确认消息</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicConsume</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">DefaultConsumer</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="nd">@Override</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Envelope</span> <span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">AMQP</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">BasicProperties</span> <span class="n">properties</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者1: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicAck</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">getDeliveryTag</span><span class="p">(),</span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">);</span><span class="c1">//手动确认消息</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <ul> <li><p>设置通道一次只能消费一个消息</p> </li> <li><p>关闭消息的自动确认,开启手动确认消息</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 357.1917808219178" data-width="2086" data-height="292"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/8b0503fcd94276ffe0b6bf29a38fcf49.png" alt="image-20200314230412178" /><figcaption>image-20200314230412178</figcaption></figure></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 506.8181818181818" data-width="2230" data-height="220"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/361040c596a40024c5a056a69e7bf299.png" alt="image-20200314230423280" /><figcaption>image-20200314230423280</figcaption></figure></p> </li> </ul> <hr> <h3>4.5 第三种模型(fanout)</h3> <p><code>fanout 扇出 也称为广播</code></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 214.07035175879398" data-width="852" data-height="199"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/f9ace2504750521640bb28c2f473a7a0.png" alt="image-20191126213115873" /><figcaption>image-20191126213115873</figcaption></figure></p> <p>在广播模式下，消息发送流程是这样的：</p> <ul> <li>可以有多个消费者</li> <li>每个<strong>消费者有自己的queue</strong>（队列）</li> <li>每个<strong>队列都要绑定到Exchange</strong>（交换机）</li> <li><strong>生产者发送的消息，只能发送到交换机</strong>，交换机来决定要发给哪个队列，生产者无法决定。</li> <li>交换机把消息发送给绑定过的所有队列</li> <li>队列的消费者都能拿到消息。实现一条消息被多个消费者消费</li> </ul> <h5>1. 开发生产者</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//声明交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">exchangeDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;logs&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;fanout&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span><span class="c1">//广播 一条消息多个消费者同时消费</span> <span class="c1">//发布消息</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicPublish</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;logs&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">getBytes</span><span class="p">());</span> </pre></div> <h5>2. 开发消费者-1</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//绑定交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">exchangeDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;logs&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;fanout&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//创建临时队列</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">queue</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="na">getQueue</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//将临时队列绑定exchange</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Envelope</span> <span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">AMQP</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">BasicProperties</span> <span class="n">properties</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者1: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>3. 开发消费者-2</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//绑定交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者2: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>4.开发消费者-3</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//绑定交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者3: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>5. 测试结果</h5> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 923.469387755102" data-width="1810" data-height="98"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/d40cecbc694fee486252253e191afa2b.png" alt="image-20200315180653207" /><figcaption>image-20200315180653207</figcaption></figure></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 974.1935483870968" data-width="1812" data-height="93"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/bc5d149cca7ce6a283a54f9eacb9629d.png" alt="image-20200315180708489" /><figcaption>image-20200315180708489</figcaption></figure></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 942.7083333333334" data-width="1810" data-height="96"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/987743f4d76ae6fe2f03c612800cb911.png" alt="image-20200315180728035" /><figcaption>image-20200315180728035</figcaption></figure></p> <hr> <h3>4.6 第四种模型(Routing)</h3> <h4>4.6.1 Routing 之订阅模型-Direct(直连)</h4> <p><code>在Fanout模式中，一条消息，会被所有订阅的队列都消费。但是，在某些场景下，我们希望不同的消息被不同的队列消费。这时就要用到Direct类型的Exchange。</code></p> <p>在Direct模型下：</p> <ul> <li>队列与交换机的绑定，不能是任意绑定了，而是要指定一个<code>RoutingKey</code>（路由key）</li> <li>消息的发送方在 向 Exchange发送消息时，也必须指定消息的 <code>RoutingKey</code>。</li> <li>Exchange不再把消息交给每一个绑定的队列，而是根据消息的<code>Routing Key</code>进行判断，只有队列的<code>Routingkey</code>与消息的 <code>Routing key</code>完全一致，才会接收到消息</li> </ul> <p>流程:</p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 206.03864734299518" data-width="853" data-height="207"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/b376d282d23be3c7012b444a15dfd2cd.png" alt="image-20191126220145375" /><figcaption>image-20191126220145375</figcaption></figure></p> <p>图解：</p> <ul> <li>P：生产者，向Exchange发送消息，发送消息时，会指定一个routing key。</li> <li>X：Exchange（交换机），接收生产者的消息，然后把消息递交给 与routing key完全匹配的队列</li> <li>C1：消费者，其所在队列指定了需要routing key 为 error 的消息</li> <li>C2：消费者，其所在队列指定了需要routing key 为 info、error、warning 的消息</li> </ul> <h5>1. 开发生产者</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//声明交换机 参数1:交换机名称 参数2:交换机类型 基于指令的Routing key转发</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">exchangeDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;logs_direct&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;direct&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">key</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="c1">//发布消息</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicPublish</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;logs_direct&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">key</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,(</span><span class="s">&quot;指定的route key&quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="n">key</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="s">&quot;的消息&quot;</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="na">getBytes</span><span class="p">());</span> </pre></div> <h5>2.开发消费者-1</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//声明交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">exchangeDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;logs_direct&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;direct&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//创建临时队列</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">queue</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="na">getQueue</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//绑定队列和交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueBind</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;logs_direct&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;error&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueBind</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;logs_direct&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;info&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueBind</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;logs_direct&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;warn&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//消费消息</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicConsume</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">DefaultConsumer</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="nd">@Override</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Envelope</span> <span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">AMQP</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">BasicProperties</span> <span class="n">properties</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者1: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>3.开发消费者-2</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//声明交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">exchangeDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;logs_direct&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;direct&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//创建临时队列</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">queue</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="na">getQueue</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//绑定队列和交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueBind</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;logs_direct&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;error&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//消费消息</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicConsume</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">DefaultConsumer</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="nd">@Override</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Envelope</span> <span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">AMQP</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">BasicProperties</span> <span class="n">properties</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者2: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>4.测试生产者发送Route key为error的消息时</h5> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 569.2567567567568" data-width="1685" data-height="148"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/5009a1d26e7f3a0f66e32682bae36668.png" alt="image-20200316102613933" /><figcaption>image-20200316102613933</figcaption></figure></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 519.8757763975156" data-width="1674" data-height="161"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/69cb52fb9950dbab04b5c0c959a86fe6.png" alt="image-20200316102627912" /><figcaption>image-20200316102627912</figcaption></figure></p> <h5>5.测试生产者发送Route key为info的消息时</h5> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 653.1007751937984" data-width="1685" data-height="129"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/119d3d4bbfb8348c0332f627120cbd72.png" alt="image-20200316102925740" /><figcaption>image-20200316102925740</figcaption></figure></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 506.6265060240964" data-width="1682" data-height="166"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/d3b2aae6a3db345ec626e694c6001abc.png" alt="image-20200316102947326" /><figcaption>image-20200316102947326</figcaption></figure></p> <hr> <h4>4.6.2 Routing 之订阅模型-Topic</h4> <p><code>Topic</code>类型的<code>Exchange</code>与<code>Direct</code>相比，都是可以根据<code>RoutingKey</code>把消息路由到不同的队列。只不过<code>Topic</code>类型<code>Exchange</code>可以让队列在绑定<code>Routing key</code> 的时候使用通配符！这种模型<code>Routingkey</code> 一般都是由一个或多个单词组成，多个单词之间以”.”分割，例如： <code>item.insert</code></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 243.55769230769232" data-width="2533" data-height="520"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/78f06c5d8a0ff5df356eb84a9117d0d9.png" alt="image-20191127121900255" /><figcaption>image-20191127121900255</figcaption></figure></p> <p>``` </p> <h1>统配符</h1> <pre><code> * (star) can substitute for exactly one word. 匹配不多不少恰好1个词 # (hash) can substitute for zero or more words. 匹配一个或多个词 </code></pre> <h1>如:</h1> <pre><code> audit.# 匹配audit.irs.corporate或者 audit.irs 等 audit.* 只能匹配 audit.irs </code></pre> <pre><code> ##### 1.开发生产者 ```java //生命交换机和交换机类型 topic 使用动态路由(通配符方式) channel.exchangeDeclare("topics","topic"); String routekey = "user.save";//动态路由key //发布消息 channel.basicPublish("topics",routekey,null,("这是路由中的动态订阅模型,route key: ["+routekey+"]").getBytes());</code></pre> <h5>2.开发消费者-1</h5> <p><code>Routing Key中使用*通配符方式</code></p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//声明交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">exchangeDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;topics&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;topic&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//创建临时队列</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">queue</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="na">getQueue</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//绑定队列与交换机并设置获取交换机中动态路由</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueBind</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;topics&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;user.*&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//消费消息</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicConsume</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">DefaultConsumer</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="nd">@Override</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Envelope</span> <span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">AMQP</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">BasicProperties</span> <span class="n">properties</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者1: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>3.开发消费者-2</h5> <p><code>Routing Key中使用#通配符方式</code></p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">//声明交换机</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">exchangeDeclare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;topics&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;topic&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//创建临时队列</span> <span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">queue</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueDeclare</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="na">getQueue</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">//绑定队列与交换机并设置获取交换机中动态路由</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">queueBind</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;topics&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s">&quot;user.#&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">//消费消息</span> <span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">basicConsume</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">queue</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">DefaultConsumer</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">channel</span><span class="p">){</span> <span class="nd">@Override</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">handleDelivery</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">String</span> <span class="n">consumerTag</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Envelope</span> <span class="n">envelope</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">AMQP</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">BasicProperties</span> <span class="n">properties</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kt">byte</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">body</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">throws</span> <span class="n">IOException</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">System</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">out</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">println</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;消费者2: &quot;</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="p">});</span> </pre></div> <h5>4.测试结果</h5> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 510.0" data-width="1683" data-height="165"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/0eae8ccbbb077ff027c5bf5c44acf3df.png" alt="image-20200316113935785" /><figcaption>image-20200316113935785</figcaption></figure></p> <p><figure class="pswp-item" style="flex: 508.73493975903614" data-width="1689" data-height="166"><img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/qq1820582487/Xuxx_Blogs@gh-pages/archives/assets/fbaa84d9b6ab86474b8d147fa1f1370c.png" alt="image-20200316114000459" /><figcaption>image-20200316114000459</figcaption></figure></p> <h2>5. SpringBoot中使用RabbitMQ</h2> <h3>5.0 搭建初始环境</h3> <h5>1. 引入依赖</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nt">&lt;dependency&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;groupId&gt;</span>org.springframework.boot<span class="nt">&lt;/groupId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;artifactId&gt;</span>spring-boot-starter-amqp<span class="nt">&lt;/artifactId&gt;</span> <span class="nt">&lt;/dependency&gt;</span> </pre></div> <h5>2. 配置配置文件</h5> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nt">spring</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nt">application</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nt">name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="l l-Scalar l-Scalar-Plain">springboot_rabbitmq</span> <span class="nt">rabbitmq</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nt">host</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="l l-Scalar l-Scalar-Plain">192.168.123.128</span> <span class="nt">port</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="l l-Scalar l-Scalar-Plain">5672</span> <span class="nt">username</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="l l-Scalar l-Scalar-Plain">ems</span> <span class="nt">password</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="l l-Scalar l-Scalar-Plain">123</span> <span class="nt">virtual-host</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="l l-Scalar l-Scalar-Plain">/ems</span> </pre></div> <p><code>RabbitTemplate</code> 用来简化操作 使用时候直接在项目中注入即可使用</p> <h3>5.1 第一种hello world模型使用</h3> <ol> <li><p>##### 开发生产者</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="nd">@Autowired</span> <span class="kd">private</span> <span class="n">RabbitTemplate</span> <span class="n">rabbitTemplate</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nd">@Test</span> <span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">void</span> <span class="nf">testHello</span><span class="p">(){</span> <span class="c1">//参数1:队列名 参数2:消息对象</span> <span class="n">rabbitTemplate</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="na">convertAndSend</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&quot;hello word&quot;</span><span class="p">);</span> <span class="p">}</span> </pre></div> </li> <li><p>##### 开发消费者</p> <div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="cm">/**</span> <span class="cm"> * @author Xuxx3309</span> <span class="cm"> * @Description hello word模式</span> <span class="cm"> *
